Japan's Financial Control Policy Towards Manchuria, Strives to Avoid Hasty Reform 33

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Finance convened a Japan-Manchukuo Financial and Economic Conference on the afternoon of the 5th because of the return of Arakawa Masatsugu, the financial advisor of the Kwantung Army, to study the financial state of "Manchukuo". According to Arakawa's report, the opinion of controlling Japan-Manchukuo finance in "Manchukuo" is radical. That is, the currency of Manchukuo, because silver coins are affected by the rise in silver prices, flows out of the country, gradually reducing its number, and Japanese gold capital flows into the country, expanding the circulation of Bank of Chosen banknotes. The function of the Central Bank of Manchuria to control finance is weakening day by day. Therefore, it wants to restrict the circulation of Bank of Chosen banknotes, unify finance with the national currency, and make the function of the central bank complete. At the same time, the Central Bank of Manchuria and the Bank of Chosen will establish a currency alliance and set a certain exchange rate to prevent the fluctuation of foreign value. However, the Japanese government still has objections to this, that is, the increase in Bank of Chosen banknotes is based on actual needs, so it is inappropriate to disregard the actual situation and suddenly withdraw the banknotes. As for the foreign value, the exchange rate between Japan and Manchukuo will not fall below equality because the central bank's reserves are mostly Japanese gold deposits. In short, Japan strives to avoid drastic reforms to prevent financial chaos. (Japan Union Telegram, 6th)

French Gold Continues to Flow to the United States 34

20th Session of the League of Nations Opium Advisory Committee Closes, All Members Unanimously Praise China's Drug Prohibition Achievements, Greater Contribution to the World Than Any Other Country 35

(Geneva) The 20th session of the League of Nations Opium Advisory Committee concluded today, passing a report to the Executive Yuan. The report outlines the situation of drug prohibition in the world in the past year, and pays special attention to the situation of private trafficking in the Far East. A special chapter is devoted to China's drug prohibition achievements. The committee's main decision is to include the issue of "what measures should governments take to seal up illegal drug manufacturing plants" on the agenda of the next session. The committee has also instructed the Secretariat to study the number of smokers and drug consumption in the world, and estimate the total output based on the total number of privately-made drug agencies that have been cracked down on so far, in order to find out how much smuggled drugs there are in the world. The committee recognizes the new drug prohibition regulations recently implemented by the Chinese government, and unanimously praises its efforts in drug prohibition. The members are particularly impressed by Chairman Chiang's vigorous and unremitting efforts in drug prohibition, and believe that Chiang has clearly understood that China's opium prohibition methods cannot be successful without major reforms. Therefore, he resolutely replaced the infeasible immediate prohibition plan with a feasible six-year prohibition plan. In addition, the reduction of opium production in Yunnan and other places, the establishment of drug rehabilitation centers, the treatment of 81,000 drug addicts in one year, and the severity of penalties have all given the committee a good impression. The committee is deeply saddened by the situation in Manchuria and Jehol, but is obviously unwilling to discuss it in open meetings. However, it is well aware of the seriousness of the situation, and the Chinese government cannot be responsible, and the impact will probably constrain the Chinese government's efforts in North China and other places. In addition, China's latest drug prohibition regulations have been scheduled for discussion at the next meeting. Some members regret that there are no statistics on drug prohibition tax revenue. In short, China's contribution to global drug prohibition in the past twelve months is greater than that of any other country, which has been confirmed, and the increase in prestige in the international arena is undeniable. (Central News Agency Telegram, 5th)

US Silver Purchase Policy Becomes Another Mystery of the Current Situation; Ministry of Finance Reduces Purchases but Congressmen Take No Action; New Proposal by Senator Walsh 36

(Washington) The Ministry of Finance has recently deliberately reduced silver purchases, yet silver bloc congressmen have taken no action. Observers today find this quite perplexing. In the past, whenever the Ministry of Finance slightly relaxed its silver purchase plan, silver bloc congressmen would immediately propose vigorous motions to compel Finance Minister Morgenthau to intensify purchases. Therefore, the recent lack of response from the silver bloc, coupled with the statements of Representatives Dies and Martin, raises further questions about the silver bloc's attitude. Well-informed sources here believe that the Ministry of Finance's gradual approach to silver is due to the following two reasons:

(1) To maintain the Exchange Stabilization Fund without using it, in preparation for the collapse of the European gold standard group, so as to adjust drastic changes in the dollar exchange rate.

(2) To allow China and other countries adversely affected by the silver purchase policy to slightly ease their situations, so that they can each reorganize their monetary policies.

Today, Democratic Senator Walsh introduced a bill advocating authorizing the Ministry of Finance to delineate the scope of silver for monetary use and silver for commercial use. This is the only expression of interest in silver in Congress. Walsh stated that the purpose of the bill is to prevent fluctuations in the price of silver for commercial use. At the same time, Finance Minister Morgenthau has amended the regulations on licenses for the import of foreign silver coins set on August 17th of last year, stipulating that only the Federal Reserve Bank of New York or government representatives may import silver coins without a license, but American silver coins may still be imported without a license. Licensees must also prove that the imported silver coins are for repayment of legitimate debts and have obtained permission from the foreign government, or are especially treasured by collectors, it is said.

Senator Walsh's proposal will not have a major impact on the United States' silver policy, as the bill does not restrict the import of silver bullion. Monetary experts believe that prohibiting the import of foreign silver coins is not significant internationally, as silver coins can be melted into silver bullion and then imported, and this method has already been implemented. It is said that the greatest value of prohibiting the import of silver coins is that it can provide cooperative assistance to countries that prohibit the export of silver coins. (5th National Dispatch)

The US Recovery Problem: A Legislative Theory to Preserve the Shell 37

(Washington) There is talk in Congress today of enacting legislation to preserve the shell of the National Recovery Administration (NRA), but this matter has not yet been finally decided, nor is it known what basis will be used to create this legislation. Addressing a gathering of New England bankers in Massachusetts today, former NRA Director General Johnson said that many resolutions passed by trade associations supporting the continued maintenance of industry standards were merely perfunctory plans, and that they would revert to their old ways after Congress adjourned. He predicted that turmoil would arise after the NRA's demise. Chamber of Commerce President Shepley praised the NRA's plan without industry standards, saying that this was exactly what the business community wanted. At the same time, the Executive Committee of the American Federation of Labor is currently meeting to discuss the NRA plan with a hostile attitude. Chairman Jones of the House Agriculture Committee stated today that the licensing methods of the Agricultural Adjustment Administration (AAA) will now be completely abolished and replaced by prudent regulations and limited authority, which will be entrusted to the Secretary of Agriculture, who will issue appropriate orders. It is said that President Roosevelt issued a warning today that if the Wagner Labor Act and the Guffey Coal Stabilization Act cannot be passed, the government may have to declare martial law to prevent riots. President Roosevelt believes that since the NRA no longer exists, these two acts are indispensable. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Anglo-German Naval Talks: Britain Tries to Narrow Germany's Demands; German Representatives Request Time to Consider and Reply 38

(London) Anglo-German naval representatives continued their talks today. According to the German representatives' previous announcement of Germany's naval construction plan, its total tonnage will account for 35% of the British Navy's total tonnage, including five battleships, sixteen cruisers, and fifty destroyers. The British side believes that the construction of five battleships may be acceptable, but the construction of many cruisers and destroyers would endanger the British Navy's dominance in the North Sea. If Germany's demands are accepted, Britain will inevitably increase its naval shipbuilding program to cope with the emerging situation. This is the main point of disagreement between Britain and Germany. During today's talks, Britain tried to narrow the scope of Germany's demands, advocating that the quality of all types of warships built by Germany should be limited. According to informal naval circles, the British representatives expressed during the talks their hope that, in terms of quality, each German battleship would be limited to 35,000 tons, cruisers to 10,000 tons, battleships would not be equipped with guns exceeding 12 inches in diameter, and cruisers would not be equipped with guns exceeding 6 inches in diameter. In terms of quantity, the British delegation advocated that Germany's shipbuilding plan should be divided into several years for phased construction. From these two proposals, it can be seen that Britain's intention and purpose are to ensure that the work of future naval conferences is not undermined by Germany's rearmament of its navy. After receiving the conditions proposed by Britain, the German representatives requested considerable time to consider and reply. Therefore, the Anglo-German talks have been postponed to Friday or next Tuesday for continuation. (5th Havas Dispatch)

(London) There has been no news for a long time about the Anglo-American-Japanese naval negotiations, and the opening of a naval conference is even more distant. It is learned that Japan has indicated to Britain and the United States that if the two countries can reduce the tonnage of each type of warship, Japan can also qualitatively limit the number of ships. It seems that naval negotiations may have new developments, which is not impossible. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Anglo-German WWI Generals Pass Away: Viscount Byng and General von Linsingen 39

(London) Viscount Byng died of internal illness at the age of 73. Doctors performed surgery on him on Tuesday, but unexpectedly it was unsuccessful. The outside world is deeply shocked by this, as the general's illness did not seem very serious before the surgery. During World War I, Byng initially led only a cavalry division, and later rose to become a general commanding 250,000 troops. All Canadian soldiers who participated in the war were under his command. In recent years, he was old and frail, so he resided in southern France and South Africa. (6th National Dispatch)

(Berlin) General von Linsingen, who served as the commander of the German Southern Army during World War I and was renowned for his achievements, died here today at the age of 85. The general retired in 1918, ashamed to wear military uniform again because of Germany's acceptance of the humiliating Treaty. Since Hitler came to power, the general was often seen attending public meetings of veterans' associations in military uniform. During the German Revolution of 1918, the general served as the commander of the Brandenburg Province. On the day the revolution broke out, the general ordered the bombing of Berlin from the air to prevent the concentration of the revolutionary party, but this order was immediately revoked by the Ministry of War to avoid unnecessary bloodshed. Thereupon, the general forbade his troops from using weapons to show his protest. Soon, his subordinates also joined the revolutionary party. The general resigned on November 17, 1918. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

The Work of Suppressing the Red Bandits and Building Sichuan 82

——Address by Chairman Chiang at the Tea Party with Gentlemen and Elders in the Sichuan Provincial Capital——

Chengdu Correspondence. At 4 p.m. on the 3rd, Chairman Chiang invited gentlemen, elders, financial magnates, and representatives of people's organizations from the provincial capital to a tea party at the administrative headquarters. A total of 64 people attended, including Fang Xu, Zeng Jian, Xu Jiong, Yin Changling, Liu Xianrong, Zhou Daogang, and Chen Guodong. Li Hongkun, Chief of Staff of the Supervisory Office and Garrison Commander, and Zhong Tigan, the mayor, were responsible for the reception, and Zhong introduced each of them to Chairman Chiang. The gentlemen and elders contributed many opinions on governing Sichuan and saving the country. Chairman Chiang gave an impromptu speech as follows: "I have been in Chengdu for a week now. I originally intended to meet with you gentlemen earlier, but I was slightly delayed due to business. Today, I have specially invited you here to discuss together and listen to your advice. I have just heard your remarks, which are all brilliant and pertinent, and can be said to be the words of truth. They have a great relationship to the future of Sichuan. Not only Sichuan, but the entire country cannot be governed without following the principles you have discussed."

The Work of Suppressing the Red Bandits and Building Sichuan in the Future

"You gentlemen have been living in your hometowns for a long time, and you have a detailed understanding of the actual situation in the area and various reforms. I don’t need to add more. There are too many things in the past, and I don’t have time to discuss them today. Let them pass with time. What we need to study most urgently is how to promote the work of suppressing the Red Bandits and building Sichuan in the future. Regarding this point, I hope that you will tell me your opinions at any time and plan together, so that the banditry can be quelled quickly, the situation in Sichuan can be stabilized early, and the people of the whole province can live and work in peace. You gentlemen expect a lot from me, but if you want to save the people of Sichuan from their dire situation and enable them to live and work in peace as soon as possible, it cannot be achieved by bringing a few troops and a few salaries. The problem in Sichuan today is not the lack of troops, nor the lack of salaries, but the depravity of people's hearts and the decline of social customs. If this cannot be revitalized and transformed, then any effort will ultimately be ineffective, and all undertakings will be hopeless. On the contrary, if people's hearts are revitalized and social customs are renewed, then the impetus for improvement will be unstoppable, and everyone will have no choice but to do good. Then, all problems in military affairs, politics, society, and economy can be easily solved. Therefore, revitalizing people's hearts and transforming social customs are the fundamental strategies for suppressing the Red Bandits and building Sichuan today. I sincerely hope that you elders and virtuous gentlemen, based on the principle of "responsibility for the rise and fall of the nation," will devote yourselves to the cause of educating the country, take responsibility, and work hard in this regard. We must first renew social customs, and then we can talk about the construction of Sichuan. If a new Sichuan can be built successfully, it will surely be a model province and the foundation for the revival of the nation, so that our Republic of China will gradually move towards unification and stability, and then towards a long-lasting and prosperous realm."

The Goal of Cultivating New Social Customs is Divided into Six Items

"There are many conditions needed to revitalize people's hearts and transform social customs. The key is that the government authorities and general social leaders can determine the goals, set an example, and work together in many ways. Now, based on what I have always encouraged myself and what you gentlemen have mentioned today, and what Sichuan Province urgently needs to cultivate in the future, I will describe six goals as follows: First, clumsiness. In terms of things, Sichuan is blessed by nature and is the richest. It must not be said to be poor. In terms of people, I believe that the intelligence of the people of Sichuan is the best in the country. However, excessive cleverness has led to many drawbacks, resulting in the current situation where they compete to seize advantages and fear falling behind, and avoid difficulties and only know how to be opportunistic, wanting to seek advantages. As a result, everyone fails and suffers. Cleverness is self-defeating, which is lamentable. Therefore, if we want to revitalize people's hearts and transform social customs today, we must first persuade the people to be clumsy. All true undertakings in the world come from honest effort and hard struggle. They cannot be achieved by being opportunistic, and there is no advantage to be gained. Moreover, things in the world are constantly changing, and people's hearts in the end times are full of tricks. We can only use clumsiness to control cleverness and use reality to break through falsehood, so that we can achieve something. Transforming social customs and saving Sichuan and the country are the top priorities. Therefore, I hope that you gentlemen will advocate simplicity for the people of Sichuan. Second, sincerity. "Without sincerity, there is nothing." "Sincerity is like a god." Establishing oneself and establishing a nation, from ancient times to the present, the first important thing is to open one's heart sincerely. Today, people's hearts are frivolous and hypocritical, and they are accustomed to mechanical deception to the extreme. Sichuan Province has been chaotic for many years, and the accumulated malpractices are particularly deep. Intrigues and infighting have become the norm. From now on, we should remove this root cause and vigorously correct the malpractices of the times, taking morality as the purpose and loyalty as the appeal. The ancients said, "Where sincerity is, even metal and stone can be opened." If our government authorities and social leaders can sincerely advocate for the people, they will surely be able to revitalize people's hearts and renew social customs in the shortest possible time. Third, public. When the Great Way is practiced, the world belongs to all. Since ancient times, only those who can open their hearts sincerely, practice justice, be selfless, and forget their families for the sake of the country can succeed in their careers and contribute to the world and the country. Today, people's hearts are depraved due to selfishness. Once selfishness exists, deception arises, and competition begins. As a result, the four virtues are not promoted, and disasters never end. The past events of Sichuan have been deeply poisoned by this selfishness. In the future, if we want to revitalize people's hearts, transform social customs, restore order, and save the province and the country, we must advocate impartiality for all the people of the province. Fourth, hard work. If you want to change customs and habits, it is important to set an example and inspire the masses. It is even more important to take the lead in hard work, to endure what others cannot endure, and to do what others do not want to do. Or avoid danger and fear difficulties, and seek temporary security. I must take risks and assume difficulties, taking self-suffering as pleasure. Only in this way can we move people's hearts and make them ashamed of fearing difficulties and seeking temporary security, and ashamed of seizing profits and abandoning righteousness, and consciously and vigorously follow me and advance towards goodness. From ancient times to the present, scholars and gentlemen who have saved people's hearts, transformed the world, settled great disasters, and achieved great achievements have all done so. I am willing to encourage each other with you elders and virtuous gentlemen. Fifth, thrift. "The failure of a country is due to the corruption of officials." The prevalence of bandits is mostly caused by greed and evil. Therefore, clean politics is an essential element for thoroughly suppressing bandits and a prerequisite for all construction. To achieve clean politics and eliminate corruption, the government must strictly enforce laws and regulations and rectify official rules. In society, it is necessary to promote thrift in order to correct the bad habit of extravagance, eliminate the psychology of indulgence, and cultivate the virtues of frugality, integrity, and uprightness. The so-called "plainness clarifies ambition, and frugality nourishes integrity" refers to this. According to the current situation in Sichuan Province, the painful lives of the majority of the people and the extreme extravagance of a small number of people have almost become two extremes. All kinds of disasters arise from this. Therefore, to quell disasters, we must rectify people's hearts and advocate thrift. Sixth, strictness. I have just heard your gentlemen's heartfelt remarks, and I am deeply aware that discipline is the most important thing today. You have cited the example of Zichan governing Zheng with severity and Zhuge Liang governing Shu with strictness. I remember that Hu Linyi once said, "Without the means of thunder, the heart of a Bodhisattva cannot be shown." "Using severity to govern chaos" is a matter of last resort. Sichuan has been chaotic for many years and has not been governed for a long time. From now on, how to clarify officialdom, rectify official rules, eliminate corruption and punish the cunning? We should implement strict policies with the most impartial heart. Government authorities and social leaders should jointly take rectifying discipline and making clear penalties and abiding by the law as the primary task of the new beginning. Then, quelling chaos in the invisible and eliminating malpractices to promote benefits will be great."

"Today, I invited you gentlemen here to meet and talk, and I am very happy and grateful to hear your advice. I would like to propose the above six characters for joint discussion. If you gentlemen agree, please use them as the guidelines for military affairs, politics, and society in the future, and work together to create a new opportunity. I also hope that we can discuss them at any time and promote them together, so that people's hearts will be revitalized, social customs will be transformed, and the construction of Sichuan and the revival of China will depend on them." (Central News Agency)

The National Capital's Air Defense Exhibition Opens Yesterday 83

—Yang Jie Reports on the Significance of the Exhibition—

Beijing News. In order to universally instill air defense knowledge among the masses, the Air Defense Committee held an air defense exhibition in the First Park. The association held an opening ceremony at the public stadium on Park Road at 9 a.m. on the 6th. The chairman of the conference was Yang Jie, the chairman of the Air Defense Committee. About 30,000 people from various ministries, commissions, agencies, organizations, representatives of military schools, all students, and people from all walks of life attended. After Yang Jie led the salute, he first reported on the significance and preparations for the exhibition, stating: "Now, the method of warfare is based on scientific progress and the development of the air force. It has progressed from a flat plane to a three-dimensional war range and has expanded from the front to the rear and local areas of the country. Therefore, air defense is the most important task in national defense today. Our country is under the watchful eyes of the powers. At this time of emergency, when a world war is imminent, we should pay attention to air defense facilities in order to reduce the casualties of air force attacks. However, our country's air defense cause is still in its infancy. It is not easy to succeed without the joint efforts of the military and civilians. This association wants to arouse the attention of the masses to air defense and try to universally instill air defense knowledge. A special air defense exhibition will be held in Beijing, using various air defense charts, models, movies, photos, and texts to show the tragic enemy air force attacks and the necessary preparations for air defense. Audiences can fully understand the importance of air defense and the advantages and disadvantages of the air force. Unfortunately, the time is tight, and all the equipment in the meeting is far from what is hoped for. The performances are childish, which is inevitable. Please forgive the audience." Next, Tang Shengzhi, the Director of Training, gave a speech, stating: "Just now, the chairman gave a detailed speech on the important meaning of air defense, and I will not repeat it. This air defense exhibition collected various air defense equipment, models, charts, and publications. Various small pamphlets provide very detailed instructions on the air defense knowledge and equipment that modern citizens should have. I hope that after the people visit, they will immediately follow the guidance of the Air Defense Committee to engage in the preparation of civil air defense equipment and actively promote air defense knowledge to the people. Do not regard it as empty talk, or even let the impressions gained from the visit disappear with the closing of the exhibition." Next, Zhang Daofan gave a speech, stating that the people of our country have too little knowledge of air defense. Sun Yat-sen advocated saving the country through aviation more than ten years ago, hoping that the people would expand their knowledge, devote themselves to studying various air defense equipment, and unanimously help the government "consolidate air defense." Next, the foreign guest Si Tuobang gave a speech, stating that all the continental military powers in the world are now paying attention to the development of the air force. Once a war breaks out, the air force will not only bomb military positions, but also the cities and important towns in the rear. If China declares war on a country with new military equipment one day, even on the first day or even the first hour of the declaration of war, enemy planes may be found over Nanjing. Complete air defense preparations are the only guarantee of safety. I hope that people in your country will unanimously understand the importance of air defense and actively engage in the construction of various air defense equipment. Next, Yuan Yeqiu and Zhou Bomin from the Beijing Municipal Party Committee gave speeches. The ceremony was then completed, photos were taken, and the meeting was adjourned.

In order to promote the people's attention to air defense, the association printed a letter to the people, which was distributed at the venue and in the urban area. The full text is as follows: "Compatriots, the evolution of modern science has reached its peak. In terms of military affairs, various forms of warfare have also evolved in sequence with scientific inventions. In the past, the army and navy fought on the front line on a flat plane. Now, airplanes and bombs are used to carry out three-dimensional warfare in the air. The scope of the war has also expanded from the front line to the rear. In the past, national defense only needed to focus on the border. As long as the border was secure, the country could be as stable as a rock. Now, it is not the case. The improvement and advancement of aircraft has reached a thousand miles a day. The flight radius can reach 2,000 kilometers. The power of various poisonous gases, bacteria, and explosive bombs can destroy humans and various buildings in an instant. Unfortunately, once a war breaks out, even if the front-line forces are strong and the border defense is solid, if the rear is not well prepared for air defense, it may be destroyed by enemy aircraft at any time and anywhere. Therefore, air defense is the most important and urgent task of modern warfare. The seriousness of the Far East issue and the urgency of the European situation are enough to show the arrival of the Second World War. All the powers are also doing their best to expand their military equipment, increase their military budget, and extend the term of military service. They are preparing for war in order to survive in the war. Our country is the center of the Far East issue and the flashpoint of this war. No matter when and where it breaks out, our country will inevitably be drawn into the vortex. All our people should work diligently and wholeheartedly to seek the soundness of national defense and air defense, and to respond to the future war. However, our country's science is known to be backward, and the general public is not clear about the importance and significance of air defense. When the air defense exercise was held in the capital last winter, a propaganda week was organized to work hard on publicity. However, as a result, there were still few people who recognized air defense as a serious issue, and most people did not pay much attention to it, and even regarded it as a child's play. It should be known that if the general public cannot fully understand air defense knowledge, it will not be easy to train the air defense organization at ordinary times. Once war comes and enemy planes arrive suddenly, they will inevitably be in a panic and suffer many unexpected damages. The damage suffered is many times greater than that of organized and trained people. In order to universally instill air defense knowledge, the Association specially held an air defense exhibition, using a variety of charts, models, equipment, pictures, and movies to show the performance of various aircraft and air defense weapons, the destructive power of various bombs, how to organize air defense intelligence monitoring and alarms, how to deploy passive air defense, how to control lighting and transportation, how to equip fire prevention and poison prevention and disinfection, and how all military and civilians should unanimously cooperate in air defense. We must ensure that the people who visit the exhibition can fully understand air defense knowledge, truly recognize how important the air defense issue is, and be vigilant in their hearts at ordinary times. Then, air defense work will naturally be easy to organize and train. Once the war breaks out and enemy planes arrive, they will not be in a panic due to the lack of organization and training at ordinary times, and suffer serious damage. This is the significance of this air defense exhibition held by the Association. I hope that the general public will not ignore it."

Songjiang: Villagers Plead for the Cancellation of the Telegraph Bureau Land Grab Case 84

Changqiao Street in Xinzhuang Town, which belongs to the county, has recently enclosed and buried 300 mu of land for the construction of a telegraph bureau. Upon hearing the news, the local farmers were panicked. On the 5th, more than 400 people gathered and went to the district office to petition District Chief Chen, requesting that he revoke the order. After District Chief Chen repeatedly comforted them, the farmers dispersed after demanding a definite reply. It is reported that the telegraph bureau was originally located in Shanghai Middle School in Lujiabang, Shanghai. After Shanghai moved to govern, Shanghai Middle School enclosed 500 mu of land in Beiqiao for construction, at 200 yuan per mu. As a result, the bureau lost its residence. After finding Changqiao Town in the county as needed for the construction of the bureau, it was submitted to the Ministry of Communications and forwarded to the Ministry of Interior for approval to enclose the land. However, the farmers in the area are all self-cultivating, and their families depend on it for their livelihoods. Even if the state gives preferential land prices, the farmers will not be able to change their jobs to maintain their livelihoods. It is heard that the land of 300 mu to be enclosed involves the ownership of more than 200 people. Once it is enclosed, each household with five members will immediately lose their jobs, reaching more than 1,000 people. It is heard that the general villagers said that if there is no definite solution, they would rather be broken jade than broken tiles.

The theft case at the Liao residence in Jiading West Gate has been detailed in this newspaper. It is heard that the lost ornaments are worth about 200 to 300 yuan. Wuxi: Urging the Collection of 440,000 in Land Taxes 86

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, recently, due to the urgent need for funds, specially instructed County Magistrate Wang of this county to collect 440,000 yuan in new and old land taxes during the cocoon season. After this announcement of the time limit, everyone must follow the assigned numbers, actively urge the collection, and hand in the taxes on time. Shortages are not allowed, and evasions are not allowed. Those who continue to procrastinate and fail to meet the required amount will be punished.

Yangzhou: Chief Clerk Wan of the General Office Disappears and Leaves a Letter 87

Wan Bingcheng, the Chief Clerk of the General Office of the Three Vaults in Jiangdu, because County Magistrate Ma worked hard to urge the collection of new and old arrears, and because of the repeated droughts in the northwest countryside, the people's debts were not easy to collect, the market was bleak, and the officials' debts were even more difficult to clear. Yesterday (4th), the day before the Dragon Boat Festival, the library limit was 1,000 yuan today (5th). Recently, he said to his deputy chief clerk, Zhao Yujiu, that he was going out to find a solution, and if it was not as he wished, he would commit suicide by jumping into the river and be done with it. Yesterday morning at about 8:00, he disappeared. Soon, a letter from the chief clerk to Zhao Yujiu was delivered by the post office. The letter lamented the difficulties of public and private affairs and stated that he could not stay in the world any longer. He asked them to remember their old friendship and have pity on his family. At about 10:00, his younger brother, Wan Wu, also disappeared. On the 5th, it was suddenly reported that Wan had taken a car to Liuwei, and then jumped into the river in between, and that a body was found in Xinhe Bay. The truth remains to be verified. It is also heard that two suicide notes from Wan were found in Wan's tomb.

Ningbo: The Security Regiment Disarmed by Bandits 88

Wenxi Town in Cixi East Township is more than ten miles away from Cicheng, and cars can reach it directly. Last night at 9:00, more than ten bandits suddenly came to the village, all holding wooden guns and other weapons. They first surrounded the Wenxi Security Regiment headquarters and seized the weapons, including four rifles and one pistol. The regiment only had one squad leader and four soldiers. They resisted for a while, but were outnumbered and were eventually disarmed. The squad leader was wounded by a gunshot, and one civilian was injured by a stray bullet. After the bandits seized the weapons of the Security Regiment, they robbed the grocery store opened by Chen, the deputy township chief. Because there was not much to steal, they also tied up Deputy Township Chief Chen. The Zhuangqiao Branch of the Public Security Bureau is thirty miles away from Wenxi. After receiving the report, Chief He Peiqiang personally led a large team of police to Changshiqiao to investigate. The Cixi County Public Security Bureau has also sent a large team to pursue the bandits.

Local News

After the Government's All-Out Relief, Silver and Money Businesses All Pass the Festival Threshold Steadily 89

The Management Committee Reviewed the Collateral of Various Money Shops Yesterday; The National Goods Alliance Visited Xu Kan to Petition for Relief; The Ministry of Finance Restricted the Import of Banknote Paper

After the end of the lunar calendar's Dragon Boat Festival (also known as the Summer Festival), silver and money businesses resumed normal operations yesterday morning. The financial turmoil has subsided after the government made every effort to stabilize it. The Money Business Supervision Committee held a meeting to review the collateral of various shops. The National Goods Great Alliance visited Finance Vice Minister Xu Kan to petition for relief. The Ministry of Finance, in order to solemnly issue banknotes, restricted the import of banknote paper. Details are as follows:

Financial Stability, Turmoil Subsides

The financial turmoil in Shanghai has subsided since the Minister of Finance, Kong Xiangxi, consulted with financial leaders to stabilize the situation, and allocated 25 million yuan in financial public bonds to relieve the money businesses. The market is stable, and public confidence is gradually returning. Savings deposits in the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Four Banks Savings, Salt Industry Bank, Silk Industry Bank, and Shanghai Bank have increased sharply. The interbank lending rate in the money market was 18% both in the morning and afternoon sessions. However, the premium for borrowing with guaranteed collateral remained at a peak of 70%.

Ministry Orders Restriction on Import of Banknote Paper

In order to solemnly issue banknotes, the Ministry of Finance restricted the import of banknote paper. Yesterday, it specially instructed the Bankers' Association and other organizations, stating, "The paper used for printing banknotes is extremely important for issuance. In order to prevent the private issuance of banknotes, any printing business that purchases banknote paper in the future must first submit it to the Ministry for approval, and then entrust the Central Bank Trust Bureau to purchase it on its behalf. We have already ordered all customs offices that, in the future, any banknote paper imported that is not purchased by the Central Bank Trust Bureau should be detained in its entirety and submitted to the Ministry for review, and should not be released without authorization. In addition to notifying the Central Bank and issuing separate orders, the Chamber of Commerce is hereby ordered to immediately inform all printing businesses to comply accordingly."

Wang Yansong Visits Kong Song Yesterday

Wang Yansong, supervisor of the Bank of China, who was appointed by the Ministry of Finance as a specialist member of the Financial Reorganization Committee, visited Kong Xiangxi and Song Ziwen yesterday to discuss relief loans for industry and commerce and measures to reorganize finances. Kong went to the Central Bank to work at 5 pm yesterday and was very busy.

Supervisory Committee Reviews Collateral

After the Ministry of Finance allocated public bonds to relieve the money businesses, the member shops of the Money Business Association submitted their collateral, such as title deeds, public bonds, and goods, to the Supervisory Committee in accordance with the valuation standards of the Supervisory Committee, and applied to receive relief public bonds. The committee held a meeting at 10 am yesterday in the money business reserve of Ningbo Road to review the collateral of various shops. Xu Kan, Wang Xiaofan, Du Yuesheng, Gu Yigu, Qin Runqing, and others did not leave until after 11 am. They immediately distributed the financial public bonds deposited in the Central Bank to various shops, and at the same time deposited the collateral in the Central Bank.

Real Estate Association Expresses Opinions

The Real Estate Association believes that land deeds account for the first place among the collateral of money businesses, and the valuation relationship is important. On the 4th, they sent a letter to the Money Business Supervisory Committee, stating, "To whom it may concern, Shanghai money businesses have recently been affected by the decline of all industries, resulting in difficult turnover. On June 3rd, the Ministry of Finance, in order to relieve industry and commerce and stabilize finances, prepared 25 million yuan in financial public bonds to maintain the situation. At the same time, the Money Business Association submitted a list of various collateral to your committee for review. It is found that land deeds rank first in the collateral part, with a huge amount. The valuation problem is very important. Since the Shanghai real estate market has been sluggish since the January 28th Incident, there have been few transactions. However, the actual decline is no more than 70% to 80% of the highest market price. When money businesses accepted real estate as collateral in the past, they did not calculate according to the market price, but mostly based on the valuation of the title deed, which was stable whether the amount was high or low. However, the world economic panic has affected Shanghai, resulting in a sudden shortage of chips. Money businesses are eager to turnover, and some have re-pledged real estate collateral to banks, with valuations only half or less of the title deed valuation, and the value of the above-ground buildings is even ignored. This is a temporary abnormal situation and does not hold real value. Moreover, Shanghai is the first commercial port in East Asia, and its future development will definitely not be a complete failure. Your committee supervises the money business, and the collateral valuation is of great importance. We intend to ask you to maintain it, and use 70% of the land deed as collateral, and also value the above-ground buildings together, in order to maintain the market and stabilize people's hearts. We hope that you will adopt this."

Various Shops Study Fundamental Solutions

After the Ministry of Finance allocated public bonds to relieve the member shops of the Money Business Association, the money shops that passed the collateral review yesterday have received public bonds for adjustment. If they need cash, they can go to the Central Bank of Shanghai, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, China-South Bank, Continental Bank, Jincheng Bank, Salt Industry Bank, Silk Industry Bank, Shanghai Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, National Goods Bank, National China Bank, and other banks to pledge the public bonds for 60% of the cash, which is handled in accordance with the ordinary cash pledge method. It is heard that various shops believe that public bond relief is a temporary solution, and now they have jointly studied fundamental solutions, such as business reform.

National Goods Great Alliance Petitions

Representatives of the Shanghai National Goods Great Alliance Committee, Gu Xiyuan, Lu Xingzhuang, and Chen Yiting, went to the Central Bank yesterday morning at 10 am to visit Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, petitioning for the implementation of loans to relieve industry and commerce. However, because Kong was not there, they changed to go again at 3 pm. They were received by Executive Vice Minister Xu Keting. The representatives stated that many of the factories of their members are experiencing a shortage of turnover, and have filled out forms to the association, requesting that efforts be made to promote mortgages and credit loans for relief. Xu said that the Ministry of Finance has handed over the ten principles for issuing loans to the Silver and Money Association to be handled jointly by the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Shanghai Bank. You can inquire about the methods from Chen Guangfu, chairman of the Bankers' Association, and Qin Runqing, chairman of the Money Business Association. As for the factories requesting relief and filling out forms, you can send these forms for a look. In the future, you can also discuss the implementation methods with you at any time. The representatives were satisfied and left.

Visits to Chen and Qin Scheduled for This Morning

After returning to the association, the representatives Gu Xiyuan, Lu Xingzhuang, and Chen Yiting immediately decided to prepare letters to visit Chen Guangfu, chairman of the Silver Business Association, and Qin Runqing, chairman of the Money Business Association, at 10 am today to inquire about the progress of mortgage loans and credit loans. The association has prepared these letters yesterday so that the three representatives can take the letters out of the association this morning.

Ministry of Finance Approves Factory Joint Association

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Joint Association previously requested its member factories to make efforts to promote factory mortgage loans. The association's standing committee member Zhang Zilian and others submitted a report to the Ministry of Finance, stating the situation and applying. Yesterday, they received approval document No. 5656 from the Ministry of Finance, stating, "Your report is known. The ten principles regarding the relief of Shanghai industry and commerce loans have been sent to the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Bankers' Association, and Money Business Association to be handled jointly. You should contact them directly for handling." This is the approval.

Two Banks Have Handled the Aftermath

(1) After the Shanghai Jiangnan Bank suspended business for liquidation, the entrusted accountant Shen Jiazhen has begun liquidation. At the same time, he is holding a creditors' meeting. Those who have registered with the accounting firm in recent days, calculated based on the amount of deposits, are about more than 10,000 yuan. (2) After the Ningbo Industrial Bank suspended business, the entrusted accountant Xu Yongzuo went to the bank's head office yesterday to handle liquidation. After General Manager Wu Zhihao left Shanghai passively, it was learned by a reporter from the New Sound Society that he was in Hangzhou. Also, the savings departments established by the two banks have paid one-quarter of the reserve to the Reserve Custody Committee in accordance with Article 9 of the Savings Bank Law.

Silk Industry Creditors Oppose Liquidation

The creditors of Shanghai National Goods Company, Tianfu, Dashengfu, Silk and Satin Bureau, etc., operated by Wu Zhihao, formed a joint creditor group and entrusted lawyers Jiang Baoli and Wu Zhengkui to issue a notice stating, "According to the above-mentioned two creditor groups, Fukang Dafeng Silk Shop and other 65 companies, representatives came to our office and claimed that Tianfu and Dashengfu Silk and Satin Bureau Joint Branch and Shanghai National Goods Company, etc., owe this shop and other goods worth more than 100,000 yuan. Unexpectedly, just as the Summer Festival was about to collect payments, Tianfu and Shanghai National Goods Company suddenly announced liquidation. Although Dashengfu is continuing to operate, it refuses to pay the debt it should be responsible for. In this autumn of the decline of the silk industry, it is unbearable to suffer night rain on a leaky house. Therefore, on June 4, a joint meeting of the two creditor groups was held at the Shangzhang Silk Industry Association. Representatives from 66 shops attended, with a total debt of more than 110,000 yuan. In addition to forming a joint creditor group and entrusting your lawyers to recover according to law, they also published a notice in the newspaper, expressing opposition to the liquidation of the bureau, etc., and requesting the bureau, etc., to pay in full. If there are still those in the same industry who have not joined, they can quickly register at the office of this group in the Silk and Satin Industry Association of Sanma Road, and the amount of debt will be handled together, in order to achieve the effect of collective efforts, etc." Based on this, a joint statement is made as above.

National Goods Company Employees Petition

One hundred and twenty employees of the Shanghai National Goods Company organized an employee aftercare association, requesting the return of savings deposits and this month's salary. Representatives have been sent to contact lawyer Wang Fuxun (Wang is the temporary manager of Shanghai National Goods Company) in recent days, but to no avail. According to the employee representatives, the Shanghai National Goods Company opened in November 1932 and will be four years old this year. Mr. Wu Zhihao has devoted his life to the national goods business, and his contribution to society is commendable. In this recessionary trend, he suffered a tragic failure, which was really forced by the environment. Mr. Wu only carried 1,000 yuan when he left this time, and has no assets. The situation is very pitiful. However, the savings deposits deducted from us employees over the years have accumulated to a total of 5,000 yuan, and this month's salary, even if calculated on a half-month basis, can also get 3,000 to 4,000 yuan. However, once the business is suspended, no money is available. The company has been responsible for recording someone. Yesterday, the employee aftercare association specially sent representatives to petition the Social Affairs Bureau, and the director of the mediation department, Wang Xianqing, received them and promised to investigate and verify.

Many Wanguo Savers Still Pledged Their Certificates

Various savers of the Wanguo Savings Association have pledged their certificates to the association for loans or withdrawals. After the turmoil occurred, although the association prepared a large amount of cash, extended office hours, and made every effort to accept and receive in accordance with the regulations, the number of savers who pledged or withdrew their certificates yesterday morning was slightly less than the first day, but it was still crowded. The French Concession patrol room specially dispatched a large number of Chinese and Western patrol officers to maintain order. Savers holding certificates were allowed to enter in batches, otherwise they were rejected.

Shipping Industry Cables Chairman Jiang to Quickly Issue Public Bonds for Relief; More Than Ten Ships Have Been Abandoned and Stopped by the Industry; If the Government Does Not Provide Relief Again, the Danger of Ruin Is Imminent 93

The Shanghai Shipping Industry Association cables Chairman Jiang, etc., saying, "To Chengdu Chairman Jiang, Nanjing Executive Yuan, National Economic Council, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Communications, In recent years, the shipping industry in our country has been extremely declining. Recently, it has been affected by the market situation, and the situation is critical. We respectfully state the reasons as follows: (1) Rural bankruptcy, industrial and commercial decline, less freight, sharp reduction in freight rates; (2) Financial tightness, silver and money industries are preoccupied with their own affairs, loans are cut off, and there is no way to turnover; (3) All expenses must be paid in cash, and income is calculated on a periodic basis, and daily expenses cannot be offset; (4) The price of Japanese coal in Dalian is six yuan per ton, and the price of Chinese coal is twelve yuan per ton. The coal used by Japanese ships has already reduced expenses by half compared with Chinese ships. Also, for all ship hardware, Dalian does not levy donations and taxes. The wages of ship employees are 20% to 30% less than in Shanghai. Also, because the Japanese gold exchange rate is low, it can save 40% compared with Chinese gangs. If Chinese ship companies set up offices in Dalian, all expenses will be saved, and Japanese ships can be reduced again. Moreover, there are Japanese government subsidies or guaranteed dividends. In this comparison, Chinese ships are even more difficult. With these points, they are trapped in a desperate situation. If this continues, in addition to bankruptcy and suspension of navigation, there is really no way to make a plan. In this position, the failure of shipping merchants is not mentioned. However, a large number of sailors are unemployed as a result, and the emperor is worried. Once you think about it, it is really endless and thrilling. Now, in the industry, due to the inability to maintain, there are more than ten ships that have been abandoned and stopped. After that, the inevitable trend is to stop the shift. The duties and feelings of the association have to make the final appeal. In the 19th year, it was reported to the government to issue shipping public bonds to save shipping merchants. Although it was reviewed and approved, it has not been implemented. In these five years, shipping merchants have tried their best to survive. Now in this environment, the urgent situation is no longer comparable to the past. If the government does not provide relief again, the danger of ruin is imminent, and the catastrophe is inevitable. It is compelled to report to the top, and must add insight, and must be able to visit and approve the original case requested by the association to advance the issuance of 10 million yuan of shipping public bonds to save Chinese ships. The shipping merchants' only chance of survival depends on this move. Otherwise, the shipping merchants will have no way to go, and they will only sit and wait to die. I beg you to consider and approve the speedy implementation. The commission is eagerly awaiting orders. Chairman Yu Hede of the Standing Committee of the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association bows his head."

Art Exhibition Antiquities Shipped to England This Morning, 93 Boxes Were Shipped on the British Ship Yesterday 95

The antiquities that our country is shipping to England to participate in the London Chinese Art International Exhibition were transferred from the warehouse of the Shanghai Office on Renji Road to the British ship Suffolk yesterday morning. The ship is scheduled to depart from the port at 7 am this morning. A reporter from the Central News Agency learned the details as follows:

British Ship Arrives in Shanghai

The British ship Suffolk arrived in port the night before last. The Shanghai Office of the Association specially requested the state-run China Merchants Bureau to rent the wharf and pay one-tenth of the rent, totaling 79 yuan. That night, Mr. Tang Xifen, the secretary of the Association, inspected the ship for a week.

Antiquities Transported to the Ship

Yesterday morning, the Association hired the Movers Foreign Company's trucks and transported them to the China Merchants Bureau wharf twice with the escort of detectives. The first time, five trucks were used, and the second time, two trucks were used. All 93 boxes of antiquities were moved and safely entered the cabin. The luggage of Mr. Tang Xifen, the secretary of the Association, and Zhuang Shangyan, the section chief of the Ancient Palace Museum, who accompanied the antiquities to London, were also moved to the ship yesterday. However, Tang Zhuang will board the ship at 6 am this morning.

Banquet for Zheng Tang

Lei Zhen, Director of the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Education, hosted two banquets at the Meiyuan Restaurant on Sima Road yesterday noon. One was to send off Zheng Tianxi, Tang Xifen, and Zhuang Shangyan, the special envoys who accompanied the antiquities abroad this time, and the other was to thank everyone who assisted in holding the pre-exhibition in Shanghai last time, such as Liu Hongsheng, Li Jinpei, and Zhao Tiezhang, who were all invited.

Reception for the Captain

At 7 pm last night, Zheng Tianxi specially hosted a banquet at the Xinya Restaurant on Nanjing Road to connect with Wei Qing and entertain Captain Manners of the Suffolk, Commander Whitaker, and other senior officers, including Perrot, one of the five British envoys specially sent to China to select antiquities. The other four British envoys went to Japan a few days ago and returned to England via the United States.

Western Press Reports: 美豐 Bank Liquidation Incident 99

美豐 Bank Has 8,000 Depositors of 40 Nationalities / 普益 Has Not Closed and Is Operating as Usual

The 大陸報 reports that Mr. He Fu, the liquidator of 美豐 Bank, 美東 银公司, and 普益 银公司, has hired Dr. Xue Laite, a former American local magistrate in China now practicing law, as the legal advisor to the liquidator. He has also hired Mr. De Fute to audit the accounts of the three companies. Mr. De will begin work with his team of auditors this morning (6th). Once the audit is complete, he will report to Mr. Xi Ermike, the Chief Justice of the American Court. A 大陸報 representative met with Mr. He Fu, the former manager of 美豐 Bank, in his office yesterday afternoon. Mr. He Fu was very busy and had met with Mr. De Fute and Mr. Ya Liangman, a lawyer representing the American creditors and some depositors of the three companies. According to Mr. He, he cannot yet predict the date when the repayments to depositors will begin, but he will announce it as soon as possible to satisfy public expectations. The repayments, regardless of the amount of the deposit, will be made on a pro rata basis. Most of the assets of the three companies are in real estate. The liquidator has the power to sell this real estate for cash to repay the depositors. However, the current value of real estate is only half of what it used to be. Many real estate holders fear that the sale of all the real estate of the two companies will have a serious impact on the Shanghai real estate market. However, an American official told a 大陳報 reporter yesterday that this concern is unwarranted. In the past five or six years, Shanghai real estate prices have soared and reached their peak. If the real estate of the three companies is sold at current prices, the market will be more stable than it was during the abnormal price surge in the past. Yesterday, the main entrance of 美豐 Bank on Nanjing Road remained locked and guarded by the police. Letters and newspapers were scattered on the ground inside the main entrance. The seals on the second floor had been removed, and all the rooms were empty. Only Mr. He Fu occupied one room, assisted by a stenographer. 美豐 Bank has a total of 8,000 depositors of 40 nationalities, with total deposits of over 8 million yuan. Its capital is 550,000 US dollars and 1.25 million Chinese yuan. Last year's profit was just under 600,000 yuan. The assets of the above three companies, including those of the 普益 Land Company, are estimated to be between 60 and 70 million yuan.

The 字林報 reports that Mr. He Fu, the liquidator of 美豐 Bank and the other two companies, spent all day yesterday in the bank's office discussing liquidation matters with local financial authorities. He has also hired Mr. De Fute as an auditor. Mr. De will begin auditing the bank's accounts with his staff at 9:00 this morning (6th). Mr. He Fu told reporters last night that he plans to issue a detailed announcement to reassure the public when the audit is nearing completion. However, this will take some time, so he asks depositors and shareholders to be patient.

The 大美晚報 reports that Mr. Xi Ermike has appointed Mr. He Fu as the temporary custodian of 普益 Land Company this morning, pending investigation of whether the company can be reorganized or whether it will be decided that the company will continue to operate under the management of the custodian. Because the company's affairs are intertwined with those of other companies, it is more convenient for Mr. He Fu to serve as the temporary custodian for the progress of affairs. According to the application for the appointment of a custodian, the assets listed on the company's books as of December 31, 1934, were worth 22,181,907.48 yuan, but the actual value is now much lower than this. The amount of liabilities on the same day was 20,937,913.20 yuan. Note that 普益 Land Company is different from the other three companies and has not been closed. It is operating as usual during negotiations with the American court. A Reuters Shanghai dispatch on the 6th reports that an employee of Citibank in this city stated today that recent rumors that the bank is financially related to 美豐 Bank are false. In fact, Citibank has never had any financial or other relationship with 美豐 Bank or 普益 银公司. Furthermore, Citibank is not a participant or founder of any other commercial firm or organization in China.

Yangtze River Six Companies Alliance: Implementing Public Sharing of Freight 100

Formal Contract Signed / Implementation on July 1st / Valid for Six Months

Chinese and foreign shipping companies have negotiated to form an alliance for Yangtze River shipping and further implement public sharing of business. This matter is of great importance. 太古, 怡和, 招商, 三北, 寗紹, and other shipping companies have held numerous meetings and discussions on this matter for several months. The discussion of public sharing methods and the consideration of various conditions have caused delays. Only yesterday did the representatives of the companies sign the alliance and public sharing agreement, approving its implementation on July 1st. This matter is of great importance to the Yangtze River shipping industry. The details are as follows:

Six-Company Alliance

The Yangtze River Shipping Alliance was originally planned to include seven companies: 太古, 怡和, 招商, 寗紹, 三北, 日淸, and the American 捷江 Company, which also requested to join and was accepted by the shipping companies. However, 捷江 Shipping focuses on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, and its business on the Shanghai-Hankou route is very small. Therefore, it declared that it would no longer join the Yangtze River public sharing. Thus, it is now publicly agreed that the alliance consists of six companies.

Signing the Agreement

The six companies have convened meetings to discuss the public sharing issue for four or five months. The companies believe that excessive business competition and plummeting freight rates can only be remedied by working together to eliminate the long-standing problems of rampant rate cutting and excessive commissions. Therefore, it was agreed that the six companies would publicly share their Yangtze River business to make up for each other's deficiencies. However, due to the large number of ships, it took several surveys to determine the current tonnage of the six companies' ships. Then, based on the ships owned by each company, a public sharing contract was drafted. Only on the 5th of this month did the representatives of the six companies formally sign the agreement.

Overview of the Measures

The six-company alliance's method involves determining the net tonnage of each company's current Yangtze River ships by testing, deducting the non-cargo tonnage from the total tonnage. The companies' freight revenue, after deducting discounts and commissions, will be used as the official rate. The official rate will be based on the net freight per ship per trip and the loading capacity. For example, if the loading capacity of each ship per trip is less than 50% of the net tonnage, then 50% of the loading capacity will be added, and then multiplied by the official rate to obtain the public sharing score to determine the freight fee that the company should receive for that ship. If the loading capacity of each ship per trip is more than 50% of the net tonnage, then 50% of the non-loading capacity will be added, and then multiplied by the official rate to obtain the public sharing score to determine the freight fee that the company should receive for that ship. In simple terms, for example, for a 1,000-ton ship, 500 tons of cargo is the standard. If more is loaded, it must be shared; if less than 500 tons is loaded, it will be compensated by ships that carry more. With this method, Yangtze River ships will never compete for more cargo.

Six-Month Trial

After the agreement was signed, the six companies agreed to implement it from July 1st. The implementation period is tentatively set for six months. If it is effective, the six companies unanimously agree to continue, then the effective period can be extended.

Ministry of Justice Instructs Jiangsu High Court to Rectify Judicial Ethics 101

The Duty of Judges Is to Expose Illegal Activities / They Themselves Should Be Pure, Noble, and Above Reproach

The Second and Third Branch Courts of the Jiangsu High Court received instructions from the Ministry of Justice yesterday, stating: "Judicial officials hold the nation's constitution and preside over the fairness of trials. However, upon investigation, most of the prosecutors and inspectors at all levels are able to perform their duties honestly and legally, but there are also not a few who are accustomed to old habits and do not strive to improve themselves. Therefore, a small number of bad elements often tarnish the reputation of the entire legal community. The courts, on which the people rely for the protection of their lives, property, freedom, and rights, cannot gain their firm belief. What a pity! Since taking office, the Minister has repeatedly admonished officials throughout the country with the four words 'honesty, clarity, diligence, and caution,' believing that the position of a judge is so noble that even this minimum requirement is unattainable. Truly, one should be ashamed to death. After several months of observation, although the patching-up is more skillful and the exposure is less frequent, judging from the unevenness of the case details and the dissatisfaction of public opinion, the decisions are questionable and the integrity is untrustworthy, often coming to attention. The President and Chief Prosecutor of the Court bear the heavy responsibility entrusted to them by the Ministry and should supervise their subordinates closely. They should set an example, work together with pure hearts, be respectful in their positions, and diligently realize the principle of the separation of powers with the spirit of the rule of law. Indeed, the duty of a judge is to expose or restrain the illegal actions of the people, and they themselves should be pure, noble, and no longer subject to criticism. If they do not respect themselves and there are illegal or derelict acts, and the Supervisors find them and file impeachment, their responsibility should be considered more serious than that of other officials. The Minister has always advocated that to govern the law, one must first govern people, and to correct things, one must first correct oneself. In this case, he will definitely punish them severely according to the law, without the slightest leniency. You should immediately comply, restrain yourselves, and instruct your subordinates to follow suit. This order is of utmost importance."

The late Zhao Tieqiao, member of the Construction Committee and commissioner for reorganizing the China Merchants Bureau, was shot and killed in front of the bureau gate on the morning of July 24, 19th year. Later, at the request of the family to bury him in Hangzhou, the Zhejiang Provincial Government was instructed accordingly. Five years have passed, and it has not yet been held. Your brother Zhongzheng bows in Jiangmiyu."

Zhao's brother Tieqian also came to Nanjing and Hangzhou from Sichuan and met with President Wang and Chairman Huang, which were very satisfactory. Once the Zhejiang Provincial Government has designated the Hangzhou location, it can be reported to the Central Government for a regular date. Therefore, Central Committee member Liao Zhongkai will also be reburied in the capital from Guangdong. It is expected that Mrs. Zhao, Ms. Huang Shenyi, will make the final decision.
