Anecdotes 178

— (Chan Chen)

In the bustling city, two processions came head-on. One procession was a military band and drummers, blowing and beating, and finally a red sedan chair with a new bride ready to be married. The other procession was also a military band and drummers, blowing and beating, and the end of the line was a black lacquered coffin containing the corpse of an old lady. Marriage is the tomb of love, and this is the best concrete symbol.

Climbing to the drying platform to watch the airshow, I thought it was much clearer and more comfortable than the people standing on the street, craning their necks to watch. Looking back, who knew that people peeking out from the ×× Building were laughing at us for standing too low. Don't laugh, friends, "There are stronger hands than the strong, and more capable people behind the capable." The people sitting in the plane are laughing at us like a group of ants.

A Way to Make Money 179

— Schoolteacher

Here, I want to record a way for a low-energy principal to make money. In S city, this low-energy principal can be a standard figure who is good at running schools. He is not good at rhetoric, not good at teaching, but good at financial management.

His fat and short body, black and delicate beard, fits the saying "Many bumps in a short man's belly." In the small school he runs, there are three hundred boarding students. Each student has to pay one yuan for barber fees and three yuan for laundry fees at the beginning of the semester. He hired a barber from the interior, paying him six or seven yuan a month, specializing in doing top work for the students. He hired two middle-aged Jiangbei maids, giving them twenty yuan every six months, specializing in doing laundry work for the students. After calculating both sides, the low-energy principal can get a net profit of at least eight hundred and up to one thousand yuan every six months from these three people.

Because he advocated the New Life Movement, he issued a notice before the holidays: All school servants' wine money will be canceled. If anyone privately asks students for rewards, they will be fired immediately once verified. On the one hand, he levied servant fees of eight jiao per person. In that way, there would be an extra income of one or two hundred yuan.

Advocating goods and implementing a cleanliness campaign are good policies for the low-energy principal to manage finances. All student books, stationery, and even daily snacks must be collected from the school store and settled at the end of the semester. They must not be purchased privately from outside the school to avoid mistakenly purchasing imported inferior goods: or hindering hygienic food. Violators will be deducted from their conduct score. In this way, the school store's business is booming and it is overwhelmed. And the low-energy principal's wallet is also "full of money."

Salt Drying 180

— Wandering Goose

Salt drying is a side business for people living on the coast.

The suitable season for salt drying is the three periods of late spring, summer, and autumn. The salt matures most rapidly in the hot summer and early autumn. In the severe winter and early spring, it is not easy to dry seawater into white particles due to the cold weather.

On the morning of every clear day, or at the specified time, the tide in the sea rises to the beach as usual. On a vast salt field below a long and wide embankment, rows of salt pans are arranged (commonly known as salt boards); the bottom layer of each pan is filled with a thin layer of sea mud. Salt farmers, men, women, old, and young, are busy working there: The boys, barefooted, carry buckets of seawater from the beach, over the embankment, and place them on the salt field. The salt husbands and salt wives then pour the water into the pans, filling each pan with five-tenths of water. After spreading the water everywhere, everyone covers and stacks the salt pans on top of each other between every two pans, or stacks them into a pagoda shape. This is because there are more pans and fewer pans, so that the sunlight can shine on the water between each pan.

Before and after lunch in the upper and lower halves of the day, when the sun is scorching fiercely, they switch the upper and lower layers of the salt boards twice. When the setting sun is setting, the water in the pans becomes crystal clear and white salt blocks. Then the salt farmers use baskets to carry the salt back, and hide the salt pans in the thatched sheds beside the salt field.

After the salt blocks are stirred, they all become loose particles. On the next morning, the salt farmers carry them basket by basket to the market or town to sell, or sell them to the salt shops.

The livelihood of the salt farmers should have been reliable, but because of the heavy taxes and donations in recent years, the price of salt has been high. Due to economic bankruptcy, even the amount of salt consumed in rural areas has decreased, so they are now in a deep abyss of suffering!

Chapter 14: Another Kind of Heart: Westerners Discuss Construction with No Regrets; Poor Scholars Plant Lovesickness

He looked at it, put it on the table, and said with a smile that it is easy to buy antiques in Luoyang and Xi'an. It is very difficult to distinguish the true from the false. Zhiqian said, "Have you been to Luoyang?" He smiled and said, "I have been there. I have been to Zhangjiakou, Suiyuan, and Taiyuan in Northwest China. This time, I also want to go to Lanzhou to see." Zhiqian said, "So, you are very interested in Northwest China." Tony smiled, "Not only me, but many American economists are very interested in Northwest China. China's air routes are increasing in the northwest, and the United States is very willing to help China in aviation." Zhiqian smiled, "You are right, a large amount of commercial aircraft are being sold to China?" He smiled, seeming to nod a little. Zhiqian said, "Are you an aviator?" Tony said, "No, I am a businessman, I manage gasoline. Two trunk lines of the Northwest Highway have just been completed, and there are already several hundred cars. In the future, there will be more cars, and gasoline will need to be supplied in large quantities. I really want to go to Lanzhou to investigate the amount of gasoline needed." Zhiqian's heart moved, and he smiled, "China is originally one of the largest sales markets in the world, but the southwest and northwest parts are not convenient for transportation, and foreign goods cannot be sold smoothly. Now, Western China is working hard to build highways, which will naturally be more developed for selling foreign goods than before. What are your thoughts on this matter?" As he spoke, he looked at Tony and smiled. Tony propped his chin with his hand, thought for a while, and then gently pressed in the air with his palm, expressing his affirmation, and replied, "Really, you are right. But things like gasoline, China does not have. If you don't welcome the import of large quantities of gasoline, what is the use of this highway?" (233)

Record of Piao Miao Fragrance 183

— Original by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Not only for various decorations, but also for clothing, the Empress Dowager also carefully selected. She has a very deep study of color tones, knowing which colors are suitable for which person, and which colors will not conflict with each other, as clearly as an artist. Therefore, before holding the morning court every day, when the eight of us female officials were all dressed up and waiting in her palace, she would often carefully look at the clothes we were wearing one by one. If she saw something that was not satisfactory, she would inevitably shout loudly:

"This robe is wrong again! Don't you even realize it yourself! Go and change it to another one immediately, go! Hurry! Remember, no other color will do, you must change to a blue one! Don't make any more mistakes! ...! Seeing what you are wearing now is really disgusting."

Sometimes, the female official who was reprimanded might not understand what the Empress Dowager meant. Although she dared not openly defy, she could not help but feel a little hesitant. So the Empress Dowager had to explain it to her more clearly. For example, she said:

"Don't you understand? When we are very happy, all colors that are too light or too obvious will disturb our thoughts even more—like the pink robe you are wearing now. Not only is its color extremely incompatible with your own face, but it will also make us viewers feel strangely glaring, so it must be changed!" (333)

Designations of Imperial Commissioner and Governor-General 184

— Wu Aibo

Yesterday, I saw these few sentences in section 323 of "Yu Xiang Piao Miao Lu" in this column: (Omitted above) Speaking of Zhang Zhidong, probably no reader does not know his great name. At that time, he was serving as the Governor-General of Huguang, but when I was a child, he had not yet achieved such a prominent position, and it seemed that he was serving as the Imperial Commissioner of Hubei Province. (Omitted below) According to the original text, the author distinguishes the Governor-General and the Imperial Commissioner as two different official positions, which is inevitably a mistake. In fact, the Imperial Commissioner is the Governor-General, and the Governor-General is the Imperial Commissioner, truly "one and two, two and one."

Why is this so? Originally, most Governors-General in the Qing Dynasty concurrently governed two provinces (there were also exceptions for those who concurrently governed three or four provinces, such as the Governors-General of Liangjiang, Zhili, and the Three Eastern Provinces). They had the authority to control the civil and military officials of the two provinces, so people called him the Imperial Commissioner, and common people often called him the Imperial Chair. This was the official system of the former Qing Dynasty, and everyone at that time knew it. However, now that the Republic of China has been established, some people are confused. Deling was a female official in the former Qing Dynasty, why is she also unclear about this matter?

There is another saying that Zhang Zhidong, in the former Qing Dynasty, was promoted internally from the Hanlin Academy and then sent out to serve as an official. The first official position he held outside was the Governor of Shanxi, and later he was promoted from Governor to Governor-General, serving as the Governor-General of Guangdong-Guangxi, Liangjiang, and Huguang. His career was smooth sailing until the end of his life, and he never held any other minor official positions. Moreover, in the Qing Dynasty, there was only the Governor-General of Huguang, and there was no Imperial Commissioner of Hubei. We should pay attention to these common historical knowledge.

Acknowledgement Wu Jun Jiren is quite experienced in raising goldfish. Last year, there was a compilation of "Goldfish Breeding Methods," with an initial edition of 10,000 copies, which were sold out. This spring, a second edition of 2,000 copies was printed, and now there are not many left. Fellow goldfish lovers who wish to obtain a copy can send a letter with a ten-cent stamp attached to Tangjiazhai, No. 4, Jinyi Road, Xujiahui, Shanghai, and it will be sent by mail immediately. I received a complimentary copy yesterday, and I hereby express my gratitude.

Small Recipes

Miscellaneous Notes on Zongzi 185

— Huang Yingdai

Schools of Thought From Qingming to the Dragon Boat Festival, in our hometown, it can be called a season for eating zongzi. Especially during the Dragon Boat Festival, every household, big and small, has to wrap some zongzi; therefore, there is a saying in my hometown, "If you don't eat zongzi during the Dragon Boat Festival, no one will send you off when you are old!" to imply the custom of eating zongzi during the Dragon Boat Festival. Residents of Shanghai also have a lively time eating zongzi during the Dragon Boat Festival, but the way Shanghai zongzi are made is completely different from those in our hometown. Originally, the so-called Shanghai people nowadays cannot represent true Shanghai people, as most of them have moved from various places, so we cannot be sure where the zongzi come from, but through our superficial exploration, we can at least discover "Guangdong zongzi," "Ningbo zongzi," and "Suzhou zongzi" categories. Ningbo and Guangdong zongzi emphasize firmness, but Suzhou zongzi are relatively more soft and glutinous, and the zongzi in our hometown are more or less the same as Suzhou zongzi. Therefore, when we eat Ningbo zongzi, we always feel they are too hard to swallow and we are not used to them. Sometimes, when we bring some zongzi from our hometown, thinking they are rare treasures, Shanghai people, who are used to eating hard zongzi, praise them endlessly when they eat ours, and distribute a few to their neighbors, east and west. Who would have thought that things would turn out unexpectedly? Not only do they not say a word of praise, but they say that our zongzi are too soft and rotten. It seems that everyone has their own preferences, and I cannot help but doubt the saying, "When it comes to taste, people have the same preferences!"

Wrapping Method My hometown of Songjiang is very particular about food. Even zongzi, except for some residents living in the countryside who are not very particular, town residents are also very particular when wrapping zongzi. In terms of the types of zongzi, the shapes include triangular zongzi and long zongzi. As for the fillings, there are red bean paste, lotus seed paste, jujube, fresh meat, ham, and preserved meat. What I want to mention here is fresh meat zongzi. The way fresh meat zongzi are wrapped, in our opinion, the most elaborate is to first cut the meat into large chunks and soak it in carefully selected soy sauce. After the glutinous rice is washed, it is drained using a strainer, and the soy sauce is mixed into the rice at any time. Then, the zongzi leaves are used to wrap it, with half rice and half meat. It should be wrapped loosely, and after wrapping, hard firewood is used to cook it three times and rest three times. After five or six hours, the zongzi are cooked. Generally, vegetarian zongzi are mostly triangular in shape, while meat zongzi are mostly long in shape. Soy sauce is not added to the rice for vegetarian zongzi. The meat in the zongzi is best with half fat and half lean, so that it is deliciously fatty. Zongzi are not easy to make; if they are not wrapped well or cooked well, there will be uncooked rice. Recently, the Sijing zongzi found on the Shanghai market are also wrapped in this way. Sijing is a town in Songjiang, and Sijing zongzi have long been famous in Songjiang. The most elaborate zongzi, in addition to fresh meat, also add chestnuts and chicken meat inside, called "chestnut meat zongzi" and "chicken meat zongzi."

How to Eat Zongzi taste best when they are eaten on the spot after they are cooked, but for the leftovers, we can heat them with boiling water or cook them in cold water every day before eating. Some people like to dip them in white sugar, while others do not, which of course depends on individual preferences. However, during the Dragon Boat Festival, the weather is getting warmer, and zongzi cannot be stored for long. If they are not stored well, they will spoil. But we also have methods to keep them from spoiling for a long time, which is to put them all in a pot and boil them every two or three days. In addition, the water used for cooking the zongzi for the first time is kept, and the zongzi are placed in this water, which can also preserve them for a few more days, but too much will also cause them to spoil.

Page 15

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

"The Clock of Life and Death" and Other Things 186

— Meng Ruo

I heard that in the center of Berlin, Germany, a "Clock of Life and Death" is now being built to show the state of population reproduction and mortality in Germany. This clock chimes every five minutes. During that time, the needle indicating reproduction reports the birth of nine people, and the needle indicating death reports the death of seven people. Offsetting life and death, the German population increases by two people every five minutes, an increase of more than 210,000 people per year.

As far as we know, there are now two countries in the world that are enthusiastically implementing policies to encourage childbirth. One is Germany, and the other is Italy. They have many ways to encourage childbirth, such as levying a small unmarried tax, holding group weddings, subsidizing marriage expenses (which directly encourages marriage and indirectly encourages childbirth), and giving bonuses to families with children (the amount of the bonus is proportional to the number of children). And this "Clock of Life and Death" planned to be built in Berlin, this unique facility, although it cannot be regarded as a method of encouraging childbirth, but its concern for the increase or decrease of the national population can be seen from this.

According to the current state of the world economy, the populations of various countries can only be reduced, and should not be hoped to increase. Because in recent years, the world economic recession has become increasingly acute, and the number of unemployed people in various countries is increasing day by day. Under these circumstances, unless the economic organization of society is fundamentally transformed, the only way is to use the method of birth control to gradually reduce the population of various countries. To encourage childbirth is very inappropriate.

However, Germany and Italy are currently taking policies that are exactly the opposite. They pay close attention to their national population problems, only fearing its decrease and not worrying about its increase. Therefore, they not only do not approve of birth control, but even implement policies to encourage childbirth. They hope to use the means of encouraging childbirth to increase the population of the country day by day. They are not at ease just with this encouragement. Like Germany, they also want to build a "Clock of Life and Death" to keep statistics on the reproduction and mortality of the national population at any time.

But in today's world economic panic, why do Germany and Italy want their national population to increase? Well, this is easy to answer. We only need to look at their intensified preparations in the military field to understand why they want their national population to increase. Naturally, to have war, one must manufacture munitions. However, it is useless to have munitions without people to use them. Because although munitions are powerful, they still cannot automatically run to the enemy's position to annihilate the enemy. Therefore, to put it bluntly, the purpose of Germany and Italy encouraging childbirth and hoping for population increase is to cultivate batches of frontline soldiers. They are rushing to manufacture munitions on the one hand and encouraging childbirth on the other, which is truly a rationalization of military preparations.

Beard 187

— Lie

When sitting quietly, my fingers often inexplicably touch the chin and caress those stiff whiskers. They have spread from the temples to the neck, so vigorously, like wild grass in spring, growing densely. Sometimes they prick my fingers with slight pain. However, a lot of idle time is spent on this simple action, and when I think about it afterwards, I can't help but laugh at my own ridiculousness.

Recently, a safety razor was discarded, and those stiff whiskers became even wilder. They almost occupied the front half of my neck, so when I stroked them, I couldn't help but want to look in the mirror to see what kind of appearance they had turned me into. Because I usually see a disheveled beggar, and what I dislike most about him are those loose and fluffy things: I think everyone has this idea, right? Would those things spreading between my chin and neck turn me into that terrible image?

I remember when I was a child in school, I liked to touch my smooth chin, take square steps, and imitate the appearance of a teacher. Children's thoughts are of course simple. At that time, I didn't envy the dignity of the teacher, but imitating that appearance meant that being a teacher was like this. Now I have indeed become a dignified teacher, and those whiskers under that smooth chin naturally spread directly to the front half of my neck. However, when I stroke them myself, I don't even have a bit of the simple thoughts of childhood, and I only feel my own ridiculousness.

Facing the window of my bedroom is a playground. After school, those innocent children are playing with a ball happily. There is one smallest student, probably he doesn't have the ability to compete with his classmates, and he is crying with a sad face in a corner of the playground. That student is in the small class, and I don't teach his books, so I can't call out his name, so I wave to him at the door of my bedroom. He stared at me for a long time, but still didn't move a step, and the lack of this exercise showed very clearly from those lively little eyes that he needed someone to sympathize with him. So, I idly thought that perhaps this was caused by the teacher's dignity? So I slowly walked to the corner of the playground and picked him up. At first, he tried to sink his body down, as if rejecting my embrace; I said many good things to him, that I would buy him a big ball tomorrow, and he smiled innocently.

When he came to my bedroom, he became lively, playing with my shoes, asking who the pictures on the wall were. Finally, he took a safety razor from the dressing table. He asked me as if surprised: "Teacher, what is this?" I told him the name, and he asked me what it was used for? I immediately made a gesture and installed the blade.

"Teacher, then why don't you shave off your beard? It's scary!"

"Are you afraid of the beard?"

"Yes! Like a savage!" He finally said the reason why he was afraid of me. (Not the teacher's dignity)

These words deeply stung my heart. This beard can no longer save my golden age, but instead makes the children afraid of me. I immediately shaved off all the whiskers and picked him up to kiss his rosy cheeks.

"Teacher, you're not scary anymore, like my dad."

He stretched out his little hand to touch my smooth chin, but quickly withdrew his hand. "Teacher, it hurts!" he told me.

Yes, although those messy whiskers have been shaved off, the stiff stubble cannot be eradicated, just like wanting to save my golden age, it will become a scary appearance tomorrow!

After that little student left, I threw away the safety razor. It is a mask, it cannot help my true appearance, and may even pull me onto a worse path.

Old Man 188

— Jingfu

Bare-chested, with a black cloth bath towel draped over his shoulders and back, two iron plates with the word "May" written on them hanging behind his buttocks, and a hole in his short pants, this is the old man Ah Shou who pushes a wheelbarrow.

Page 16

From afar, he looks like a trembling patient, not standing very steadily; however, if you look closely, you can clearly see that his two withered feet are concentrating all their strength and energetically holding it up. However, his whole body is trembling with bloating, showing dark bluish-green veins, without a single piece of smooth and tender muscle. The calves of his feet, especially showing overwork, look like a bent cane.

He is so dark that he looks like a black person born under the equator! This is also a trace of prolonged exposure to the scorching sun.

His hair is sparse, half black and half white, with a full face of unevenly growing, messy weed-like beard. This old fellow also comes out with people early in the morning to find business opportunities.

A coolie like this is often unsaleable.

However, today he is very happy to have made a deal.

He can be considered a lucky one. He wasn't snatched away by his companions. He and a young man were hired together. Shaking off his withered and tired energy, the old man is very calm and careful, and he puts all his strength into it. Finally, he has piled a lot of things on the wheelbarrow. Under the urging of the employer and the grumbling of his companion to hurry up, he takes a few breaths, congratulating himself that his work has safely started.

If you focus on watching his unceasing progress by his side, you will really sweat for him. The young man is sitting in a rickshaw following his master, and he has already run several yards ahead, constantly turning his head and shouting anxiously: "Hurry up! What are you doing?" "Hey, hey," hurry up, it's just a little bit of the road," they are really too impatient to walk and wait, and their tone gradually becomes anxious: "If you can't push it, I'll hire someone else, it's really unlucky to hire this dead man!"

The old man's whole body veins are swollen and trembling as if they are about to crack, and beads of sweat are dripping like rain. Sometimes they flow from his forehead into his eyes, but he is anxious and can't even wipe them off. Because his hands and body are tightly gripping the handlebars, like the end, and his body cannot let it tilt. If his hands or body relax even a little, the car will tilt and everything will fall down with a crash. He struggles with all his strength, like dragging a treasure that is about to fall, so focused on his work; he can't even loosen his mouth to catch his breath, and he can't answer the shouts ahead, he is just anxious.

"Dead man, dead man, hire another one." These words further hit the already difficult-to-support, exhausted old man's energy, causing him to have several bouts of dizziness, and his whole body becomes even more fiery and lacks strength. However, he tries his best to endure, still panting urgently, and struggling even more to carry out his work, and the veins and skinny flesh of his whole body tremble even more severely. Pushing, pushing, if he doesn't push, he will go hungry.

When the car is pushed to the place where he has to go down the high and sloping place from the bridge, the old man's heart beats so hard that even his hands and feet are unbearably sore. The people in front shout loudly to be careful, he can only risk pushing down with his last strength, trembling, almost as if he is about to fall down, and he is a little dizzy. Just as he is about to reach the flat road, the heavy force of pushing down from above is like dragging him, making him unable to hold on any longer. His own body and the car are trembling, his strength is exhausted, his hand softens, and the things fall down with a crash, and the sound of the mirror breaking echoes, and his eyes go black for a moment.

The owner jumps out of the car and rushes over, and slaps him in the face: "Damn it, see how you pay for it with your old life." The old man trembles and can't speak. After arguing for a while, they still didn't take his old life, and hired another one. Finally, they slap him in the face again: "You didn't take your life and you still want money! Really unlucky, met a ghost!" The old man, whose energy is exhausted, falls back and sits down with sore legs.

Letter to the Editor 192

To the esteemed Editor:

I am writing regarding the singing program of the Xingguang (Starlight) Society advertised in your newspaper, which listed my younger sisters, Wang Dandan and Wang Xiaodan, as performers. My sisters have never joined any singing group of a commercial nature, nor have they ever performed for the Xingguang Society as guest singers. It is highly inappropriate for the society to include my sisters' names in advertisements published in your newspaper, causing confusion among listeners. In addition to sending a separate letter to the society to address this issue, I respectfully request that your esteemed newspaper grant a correction.

With utmost gratitude,

Respectfully submitted,

Wang Xiaolin, your brother (signed), 5th day
